< name>
Janel Quoc<//name>
<Time>1552878672667</Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I've been going to Pamper since they opened two years ago, and have consistently had positive experiences. I've had my nails done here by former employees and current employees, and the customer service skills that Vivian (the owner) imparts to all her employees is top-notch. I've always been treated like a valued customer here by everyone here, and I feel like the girls really get me and understand what I want done on my nails. Currently Jas is my go-to nail artist, and she never fails to create absolute magic with my nails.

Pamper Nail Gallery is for people who appreciate nail art, want something unique, and have patience and understanding for the hard work artists put into their craft to create something special for you. So, yes, it's more expensive than your local neighborhood shop, but these girls sculpt your nails out of acrylic or hard gel (your choice but I'm partial to acrylic), and don't use tips. Also, I used to go to other nail shops too, but I've never seen as many glitters, foils, stones, special gel polishes, shimmer pigments, etc., at any other place than Pamper. And yes, it takes longer to sculpt nails than to use tips, but sculpting allows for the structure of the nail to be more sound as it truly fits your unique nail bed. (Case in point: I get long and sometimes extra long nails, and I work in the tech industry so I'm typing all day. I also do dishes and clean like we all do, and haven't had a nail break in these 2 years coming to Pamper.)

TLDR: If you're in the market for a shop that can make your wildest (and tamest) nail art dreams come true, I think Pamper is the number one place to do it.</text>

Please note I grew up in a nail salon and know how to do nails myself, I just choose to get them done because I enjoy pampering myself, which by the way, this place doesnt live up to its name. When you arrive, you have to go up to the receptionist, if not they will not acknowledge you. All the techs have a sense of entitlement about them, and dont really care for customer service, like they just want to finish and get you out so they can go back to gossiping with one another. This is a good Mexican type grocery store,where anybody in the world is welcomed.they make fresh sweetbread every day,alot of different flowers and shapes.they make fresh flowers and corn tortillas daily.they also make different type of hot food for taking out or you could eat in there ,they have nice bathrooms for any one to use.they have tables and chairs for  anyone to use.they make different types ,flavors of cakes,for birthday,etc.you just have to order it in advance.they make tortillas like for wedding or parties etc. You just have to order in advance and store makes them for when you want or need,they sell anything a grocery store sells and fruit and vegetables and different types of meats,and different Mexican cheeses and cremas.they have little section where you can send or receive money to places all over world,good service.theres another section where the sell jewelry.very good store try it and see.</Review>
